			left join r_t_po rpo on (rpo.id = rso.po_id)
			left join m_cv c on (rso.cv_id = c.id)
            left join m_customers cs on (rso.customer_id = cs.id)
			left join users u on (rso.marketing_id = u.id)
			where rso.id = favicon.ico
